21        we used, and condensing that into practical, usable                          21                           on Thursday, 16 May 2024)
22        advice and guidance and then supervising that through                        22
23        the 24-hour command and control system that we had.                          23
24        Again, I think that was successful but it was very, very                     24
25        difficult work.                                                              25
